org.apache.kafka.common.config.ConfigDef.ValidString.in;\n83: import static org.apache.kafka.common.config.ConfigDef.parseType;\n84: \n85: /**\n86:  * Configuration for a {@link KafkaStreams} instance.\n87:  * Can also be used to configure the Kafka Streams internal {@link KafkaConsumer}, {@link KafkaProducer} and {@link Admin}.\n88:  * To avoid consumer/producer/admin property conflicts, you should prefix those properties using\n89:  * {@link #consumerPrefix(String)}, {@link #producerPrefix(String)} and {@link #adminClientPrefix(String)}, respectively.\n90:  * <p>\n91:  * Example:\n92:  * <pre>{@code\n93:  * // potentially wrong: sets \"metadata.max.age.ms\" to 1 minute for producer AND consumer\n94:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\n95:  * streamsProperties.put(ConsumerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG, 60000);\n96:  * // or\n97:  * streamsProperties.put(ProducerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG, 60000);\n98:  *\n99:  * // suggested:\n100:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\n101:  * // sets \"metadata.max.age.ms\" to 1 minute for consumer only\n102:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.consumerPrefix(ConsumerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG), 60000);\n103:  * // sets \"metadata.max.age.ms\" to 1 minute for producer only\n104:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.producerPrefix(ProducerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG), 60000);\n105:  *\n106:  * StreamsConfig streamsConfig = new StreamsConfig(streamsProperties);\n107:  * }</pre>\n108:  *\n109:  * This instance can also be used to pass in custom configurations to different modules (e.g. passing a special config in your customized serde class).\n110:  * The consumer/producer/admin prefix can also be used to distinguish these custom config values passed to different clients with the same config name.\n111:  * * Example:\n112:  * <pre>{@code\n113:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\n114:  * // sets \"my.custom.config\" to \"foo\" for consumer only\n115:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.consumerPrefix(\"my.custom.config\"), \"foo\");\n116:  * // sets \"my.custom.config\" to \"bar\" for producer only\n117:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.producerPrefix(\"my.custom.config\"), \"bar\");\n118:  * // sets \"my.custom.config2\" to \"boom\" for all clients universally\n119:  * streamsProperties.put(\"my.custom.config2\", \"boom\");\n120:  *\n121:  * // as a result, inside producer's serde class configure(..) function,\n122:  * // users can now read both key-value pairs \"my.custom.config\" -> \"foo\"\n123:  * // and \"my.custom.config2\" -> \"boom\" from the config map\n124:  * StreamsConfig streamsConfig = new StreamsConfig(streamsProperties);\n125:  * }</pre>\n126:  *\n127:  *\n128:  * When increasing {@link ProducerConfig#MAX_BLOCK_MS_CONFIG} to be more resilient to non-available brokers you should also\n129:  * increase {@link ConsumerConfig#MAX_POLL_INTERVAL_MS_CONFIG} using the following guidance:\n130:  * <pre>\n131:  *     max.poll.interval.ms &gt; max.block.ms\n132:  * </pre>\n133:  *\n134:  *\n135:  * Kafka Streams requires at least the following properties to be set:\n136:  * <ul>\n137:  *  <li>{@link #APPLICATION_ID_CONFIG \"application.id\"}</li>\n138:  *  <li>{@link #BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG \"bootstrap.servers\"}</li>\n139:  * </ul>\n140:  *\n141:  * By default, Kafka Streams does not allow users to overwrite the following properties (Streams setting shown in parentheses):\n142:  * <ul>\n143:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#GROUP_ID_CONFIG \"group.id\"} (&lt;application.id&gt;) - Streams client will always use the application ID a consumer group ID</li>\n144:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG \"enable.auto.commit\"} (false) - Streams client will always disable/turn off auto committing</li>\n145:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG \"partition.assignment.strategy\"} (<code>StreamsPartitionAssignor</code>) - Streams client will always use its own partition assignor</li>\n146:  * </ul>\n147:  *\n148:  * If {@link #PROCESSING_GUARANTEE_CONFIG \"processing.guarantee\"} is set to {@link #EXACTLY_ONCE_V2 \"exactly_once_v2\"},\n149:  * Kafka Streams does not allow users to overwrite the following properties (Streams setting shown in parentheses):\n150:  * <ul>\n151:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ISOLATION_LEVEL_CONFIG \"isolation.level\"} (read_committed) - Consumers will always read committed data only</li>\n152:  *   <li>{@link ProducerConfig#ENABLE_IDEMPOTENCE_CONFIG \"enable.idempotence\"} (true) - Producer will always have idempotency enabled</li>\n153:  * </ul>\n154:  *\n155:  * @see KafkaStreams#KafkaStreams(org.apache.kafka.streams.Topology, Properties)\n156:  * @see ConsumerConfig\n157:  * @see ProducerConfig\n158:  */\n159: public class
